 rajg sanyojak or janata dal (yu) ke adhyaksh sharad yadav ne baithak ke baad samvaadadaataaon se kaha ki endie ke mukhyamantriyon kii baithak jald bulaai jaaegi
 He said, "the allies of the alliance held detailed talks on the presidential election and decided that Advani would interact with all the constituents before the next meeting of the NDA to take a decision
" " Yadav said, "advani will hold talks with chief ministers and other parties of nda-ruled states
 is sambandh main nirnay lene ke liye kuch samay baad endie kii baithak phir hogi
 Those outside Delhi will also be consulted
 " Yadav, however, said that the vice-presidential election was not discussed in the meeting
 uparashtrapati kaa chunaav is varsh baad main hone vaala he
 Top leaders of JD (U), Shiromani Akali Dal, Haryana Janhit Congress (HJC) and BJP participated in the two-hour meeting at Advani's residence
 in netaaon main adwani or yadav ke alaava bhaajapa adhyaksh nitin gadakari, bhaajapa netaa sushamaa swaraj va arun jetali, purv kendriya mantri jaswant singh, jad (you) ke shivanand tiwari, shiromani akali dal ke naresh gujral or janata party ke subrahmanyam swami shaamil the
 The Shiv Sena did not participate in the meeting, as it is probably angry about the NDA not immediately taking a decision on the presidential election
 shiv sena sambhavat: pie sangama ko rajg dwaara samarthan die jane ke bhi khilaaf he, jinhen ol india anna dravid munetra kadgam (ediemke) kii pramukh je
 Jayalalithaa and Biju Janata Dal (BJD) chief Naveen Patnaik have offered as candidates
 shiv sena netaa sanjay raut se unke rukh ke bare main puche jane par unhone kaha, "is mudde par party pramukh bal thakare faisla lenge
 " pichley raashtrapati chunaav main shiv sena bhaajapa ke khilaaf chali gai thi or usne congress kii ummidavaar pratibha patil ko samarthan diya tha, kyonki vah maharashtra se hai
 BJP sources said that Advani and Sushma Swaraj had suggested the name of former Lok Sabha Speaker PA Sangma in the meeting held on Saturday
 unhone sangama se trinmul congress pramukh mamata banerjee se baatcheet karne ko kaha tha
 Sources said the party would also hold talks with Mamata and YSR Congress founder Jaganmohan Reddy on the issue
 bhaajapa kaa lakshya in dalon se rishte majboot kar bhavishya main unhen rajg main shaamil karnaa he
 The comments endie ke ek netaa ne kaha, "ham gaiyr-congress dalon se paraamarsh karenge
 Keeping the upcoming Lok Sabha elections in mind, it is our goal to strengthen their relationship
 " It is noteworthy that the ruling UPA at the Center has announced Pranab Mukherjee as its candidate
 matdaan 19 july ko hona he, jiske liye namakan patr 30 june tak daakhil kiya jayega
 'who will be the next President of the country is yet to be decided', says BJP spokesperson Shahnawaz Hussain
 matlab bijepi kii taraf se saaf ishaara he ki vah pranab mukherjee ke khilaaf ummidavaar tay karne kii koshish main juty he
 The BJP believes that it is not going to get any political benefit by standing with the government and its finance minister, during the tenure of the UPA government, which is entangled in the morass of corruption and inflation in the country
 endie ke ghatak dalon kii qareeb do ghante chali baithak main is baat par faisla nahin ho sakaa he ki pranab mukherjee ke khilaaf ummidavaar utaara jaae yaa nahin
 According to the information from the sources, the JD (U) and the Akali Dal are insisting on not fielding candidates
 lekin bijepi pranab mukherjee ko walkover dene ke khilaaf he
 'pranab Mukherjee is a good man' and 'given his political stature and experience, a candidate should not be fielded against him' - bjp's argument on such coming statements is that 'atal Bihari Vajpayee is also a good person and of high political standing
 But in the parliamentary elections, the Congress has also fielded candidates against them '
 sutron se mil rahi jaankaree ke mutabiq bijepi ne philhal apije abdul kalam ko ummidavaar banane kaa vichaar chhod diya he kyonki kalam ne ummidavaari ke liye apana naam dene ke pehle jeet kaa aankada apane paksh main dikhaane kii maang kii he jo ki bijepi yaa endie abhi dikhaa paane kii haalat main nahin he
 Therefore, now the whole Daromdar PA rests on Sangma
 pie sangama ke peeche apni taaqat lagaana bijepi ko munasib isliye lag rahaa he kyonki sangama ko bijedy or ediemke kaa samarthan pehle se hasil he
 The BJP hopes that by bringing Jayalalithaa, Naveen Patnaik and Mamta all on one platform, the NDA can be enlarged in the coming days
 sutron ke mutabiq sangama ke samarthan main mamata banerjee ke aane kii sambhaavnaaen tatoli ja raheen hai taaki sangama kii ummidavaari ko or majbooti di ja sake
 But the difficulty is coming from JD (U) and especially from Nitish Kumar
 shanivaar ko hi jedy(you) ke varisht netaa shivanand tiwari ne apni vyaktigat raay jataate hue pranab mukherjee ke paksh main sarvasammati banane kii baat kii thi
 According to sources, Nitish Kumar also wants the same
 isliye endie kii baithak main adwani ko yah zimmedaari saunpi gai ki vah nitish kumaar or prakaash singh badal se baat kar unako ummidavaar utaarne ke liye raji karne kii koshish karen

 He said, "the allies of the alliance held detailed talks on the presidential election and decided that Advani would interact with all the constituents before the next meeting of the NDA to take a decision
" " Yadav said, "advani will hold talks with chief ministers and other parties of nda-ruled states
 is sambandh main nirnay lene ke liye kuch samay baad endie kii baithak phir hogi

 NDA convenor and Janata Dal (U) president Sharad Yadav told reporters after the meeting that a meeting of NDA chief ministers would be called soon
 unhone kaha, "gathbandhan ke sahyogiyon ne raashtrapati chunaav par vistrut baatcheet kii or tay kiya ki nirnay lene ke liye endie kii agali baithak hone se pehle adwani sabhi ghatakon se baatcheet karenge

 " In the last presidential election, Shiv Sena went against the BJP and supported Congress candidate Pratibha Patil as she is from Maharashtra

 unhone sangama se trinmul congress pramukh mamata banerjee se baatcheet karne ko kaha tha

 matdaan 19 july ko hona he, jiske liye namakan patr 30 june tak daakhil kiya jayega

 bijepi ko ummid he ki jayalalita, naveen patnayak or mamata sabko ek platform par laane se aane vaale dinon main endie kaa kunba bada kiya ja saktaa he
 According to sources, the possibility of Mamata Banerjee coming in support of Sangma is being explored so that Sangma's candidature can be strengthened further
 lekin mushkil jedy(you) or khaastaur par nitish kumaar kii taraf se aa rahi he
